Became embroiled in infighting in Umayyad controlled Morroco and later reconciled with his nephew. Led to Maghrawa invasion of Western Algeria (Tahert) to punish the recalcitrant Abu'l-Bahar. #masmuda - Almohads (actually from the Kumya tribe of the butr)
#Characters: 1228885 - 1228899

	name="Yusuf" #1163-1184
